: O

DECIPHER O
, O

- O
based O

to O

. O

DECIPHER O

The O

( O

_ O

) O

( O

) O

( O
1 O
. O
3 O
% O
and O
1 O

_ O

- O

among O

( O
< O
0 O
. O

) O
. O

was O

transcription O
in O
the O
early O
events O
after O
mucosal O
injury O
has O
not O

in O

. O

We O
examined O
gene O

using O

following O

( O

) O
in O

A O

~ O

was O

( O

) O

2 O
- O

showed O

- O

to O
inflammatory O

and O

. O

Network O
- O
based O

and O

kernel O

algorithm O
demonstrated O
highly O

that O

compared O
to O

. O

Similar O

from O

substantial O

In O

, O
similar O

. O

We O
demonstrate O
that O

transcription O
signature O
after O

and O

that O
are O

airway O

. O

Gene O
expression O
occurs O
quickly O
after O
injury O
and O
is O
more O
profound O
in O
differentiated O

and O
is O

. O

Our O
data O

that O

response O
to O
injury O

in O

, O

. O

Psychosocial O
interventions O
for O
alcohol O

among O
problem O
drug O
users O
: O
protocol O
for O
a O

study O
in O
primary O
care O
. O

Alcohol O
use O
is O
an O
important O
issue O
among O
problem O
drug O
users O
. O

Although O
screening O
and O
brief O
intervention O
( O

) O

, O

among O

. O

The O

for O

and O

in O

. O

This O

aims O
to O
evaluate O

of O
the O

in O
reducing O
the O
proportion O
of O

in O

. O

Practices O
( O

= O

Regulation O

Controlled O

Nonalcoholic O

( O

) O

Our O
